     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Culture">
       Culture
      </span>
     </h2>
     <div class="hatnote" role="note">
      Main articles:
      <a href="/wiki/Culture_of_Nepal" title="Culture of Nepal">
       Culture of Nepal
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/Music_of_Nepal" title="Music of Nepal">
       Music of Nepal
      </a>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Manisha_Koirala_still2.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="900" data-file-width="600" height="330" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Manisha_Koirala_still2.jpg/220px-Manisha_Koirala_still2.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Manisha_Koirala_still2.jpg/330px-Manisha_Koirala_still2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Manisha_Koirala_still2.jpg/440px-Manisha_Koirala_still2.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Manisha_Koirala_still2.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        The Nepalese actress and
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UN_Goodwill_Ambassador" title="UN Goodwill Ambassador">
         UN Goodwill Ambassador
        </a>
        <a href="/wiki/Manisha_Koirala" title="Manisha Koirala">
         Manisha Koirala
        </a>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      Folklore is an integral part of Nepali society. Traditional stories are rooted in the reality of day-to-day life, tales of love, affection and battles as well as demons and ghosts and thus reflect local lifestyles, culture, and beliefs. Many Nepali folktales are enacted through the medium of dance and music.
     </p>
     <p>
      Most houses in the rural lowlands of Nepal are made up of a tight
      <a href="/wiki/Bamboo" title="Bamboo">
       bamboo
      </a>
      framework and walls of a mud and cow-dung mix. These dwellings remain cool in summer and retain warmth in winter. Houses in the hills are usually made of unbaked bricks with thatch or tile roofing. At high elevations construction changes to stone masonry and slate may be used on roofs.
     </p>
     <p>
      <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_Nepal" title="Flag of Nepal">
       Nepal's flag
      </a>
      is the only national flag in the world that is not rectangular in shape.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-177">
       <a href="#cite_note-177">
        [177]
       </a>
      </sup>
      The constitution of Nepal contains instructions for a geometric construction of the flag.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-178">
       <a href="#cite_note-178">
        [178]
       </a>
      </sup>
      According to its official description, the red in the flag stands for victory in war or courage, and is also the colour of the
      <a href="/wiki/Rhododendron" title="Rhododendron">
       rhododendron
      </a>
      , the national flower of Nepal. Red also stands for aggression. The flag's blue border signifies peace. The curved moon on the flag is a symbol of the peaceful and calm nature of Nepali, while the sun represents the aggressiveness of Nepali warriors.
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Holidays_and_festivals">
       Holidays and festivals
      </span>
     </h3>
     <div class="hatnote" role="note">
      Main article:
      <a href="/wiki/List_of_festivals_in_Nepal" title="List of festivals in Nepal">
       List of festivals in Nepal
      </a>
     </div>
     <p>
      With
      <a href="/wiki/Public_holidays_in_Nepal" title="Public holidays in Nepal">
       36 days a year
      </a>
      , Nepal is the country with most
      <a href="/wiki/Public_holiday" title="Public holiday">
       public holidays
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-179">
       <a href="#cite_note-179">
        [179]
       </a>
      </sup>
      The Nepali year begins in 1st of
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Baisakh" title="Baisakh">
       Baisakh
      </a>
      in official
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hindu_Calendar" title="Hindu Calendar">
       Hindu Calendar
      </a>
      of the country, the
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bikram_Sambat" title="Bikram Sambat">
       Bikram Sambat
      </a>
      which falls in mid-April and is divided into 12 months. Saturday is the official weekly holiday. Main annual holidays include the National Day, celebrated on the birthday of the king (28 December), Prithvi Jayanti (11 January), Martyr's Day (18 February), and a mix of Hindu and Buddhist festivals such as
      <a href="/wiki/Dashain" title="Dashain">
       Dashain
      </a>
      in autumn,
      <i>
       <a href="/wiki/Tihar_(festival)" title="Tihar (festival)">
        tihar
       </a>
      </i>
      in mid-autumn and
      <a href="/wiki/Chhath" title="Chhath">
       Chhath
      </a>
      in late autumn. During
      <a href="/wiki/Swanti_(festival)" title="Swanti (festival)">
       Swanti
      </a>
      , the Newars perform the
      <a href="/wiki/Mha_Puja" title="Mha Puja">
       Mha Puja
      </a>
      ceremony to celebrate New Year's Day of the lunar calendar
      <a href="/wiki/Nepal_Sambat" title="Nepal Sambat">
       Nepal Sambat
      </a>
      . Most of the festivals in Nepal are Hindu.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Festivals_of_Nepal_172-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Festivals_of_Nepal-172">
        [172]
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Cuisine">
       Cuisine
      </span>
     </h3>
     <div class="hatnote" role="note">
      Main article:
      <a href="/wiki/Nepalese_cuisine" title="Nepalese cuisine">
       Nepalese cuisine
      </a>
     </div>
     <p>
      The staple Nepali meal is
      <i>
       <a href="/wiki/Dal_bhat" title="Dal bhat">
        dal bhat
       </a>
      </i>
      .
      <i>
       Dal
      </i>
      is a lentil soup, and is served over
      <i>
       bhat
      </i>
      (boiled rice), with
      <i>
       tarkari
      </i>
      (curried vegetables) together with
      <i>
       achar
      </i>
      (pickles) or
      <i>
       chutni
      </i>
      (spicy condiment made from fresh ingredients). It consists of non-vegetarian as well as vegetarian items. Mustard oil is a common cooking medium and a host of spices, including cumin, coriander, black pepper, sesame seeds, turmeric, garlic, ginger, methi (fenugreek), bay leaves, cloves, cinnamon, chilies and mustard seeds are used in cooking.
      <a href="/wiki/Momo_(dumpling)" title="Momo (dumpling)">
       Momo
      </a>
      is a type of steamed dumpling with meat or vegetable fillings, and is a popular fast food in many regions of Nepal.
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">
       Sports
      </span>
     </h3>
     <div class="hatnote" role="note">
      Main article:
      <a href="/wiki/Sports_in_Nepal" title="Sports in Nepal">
       Sports in Nepal
      </a>
     </div>
     <p>
      Association football is
      <a href="/wiki/Football_in_Nepal" title="Football in Nepal">
       the most popular sport in Nepal
      </a>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-180">
       <a href="#cite_note-180">
        [180]
       </a>
      </sup>
      and was first played during the
      <a href="/wiki/Rana_dynasty" title="Rana dynasty">
       Rana dynasty
      </a>
      in 1921.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-181">
       <a href="#cite_note-181">
        [181]
       </a>
      </sup>
      The one and only international stadium in the country is the
      <a href="/wiki/Dasarath_Rangasala_Stadium" title="Dasarath Rangasala Stadium">
       Dasarath Rangasala Stadium
      </a>
      where the
      <a href="/wiki/Nepal_national_football_team" title="Nepal national football team">
       national team
      </a>
      plays its home matches.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-182">
       <a href="#cite_note-182">
        [182]
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      <a href="/wiki/Cricket" title="Cricket">
       Cricket
      </a>
      has
      <a href="/wiki/Cricket_in_Nepal" title="Cricket in Nepal">
       been gaining popularity since the last decade
      </a>
      . Since the establishment of the
      <a href="/wiki/Nepal_national_cricket_team" title="Nepal national cricket team">
       national team
      </a>
      , Nepal has played its home matches on the
      <a href="/wiki/Tribhuvan_University_International_Cricket_Ground" title="Tribhuvan University International Cricket Ground">
       Tribhuvan University International Cricket Ground
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cricktarchv_183-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-cricktarchv-183">
        [183]
       </a>
      </sup>
      The national team has since won the
      <a href="/wiki/2012_ICC_World_Cricket_League_Division_Four" title="2012 ICC World Cricket League Division Four">
       2012 ICC World Cricket League Division Four
      </a>
      and the
      <a href="/wiki/2013_ICC_World_Cricket_League_Division_Three" title="2013 ICC World Cricket League Division Three">
       2013 ICC World Cricket League Division Three
      </a>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-184">
       <a href="#cite_note-184">
        [184]
       </a>
      </sup>
      simultaneously hence qualifying for
      <a href="/wiki/2014_Cricket_World_Cup_Qualifier" title="2014 Cricket World Cup Qualifier">
       2014 Cricket World Cup Qualifier
      </a>
      . They also qualified for the
      <a href="/wiki/2014_ICC_World_Twenty20" title="2014 ICC World Twenty20">
       2014 ICC World Twenty20
      </a>
      in Bangladesh.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-185">
       <a href="#cite_note-185">
        [185]
       </a>
      </sup>
      On 28 June 2014, the
      <a href="/wiki/International_Cricket_Council" title="International Cricket Council">
       ICC
      </a>
      awarded
      <a href="/wiki/Twenty20_International" title="Twenty20 International">
       T20I
      </a>
      status to Nepal, who took part and performed exceptionally well in the
      <a href="/wiki/2014_ICC_World_Twenty20" title="2014 ICC World Twenty20">
       2014 ICC World Twenty20
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Results_of_ICC_Board_meeting_in_Melbourne_186-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Results_of_ICC_Board_meeting_in_Melbourne-186">
        [186]
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Nepal.2C_Netherlands_get_T20_international_status_187-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Nepal.2C_Netherlands_get_T20_international_status-187">
        [187]
       </a>
      </sup>
      Nepal had already played three
      <a href="/wiki/Twenty20_International" title="Twenty20 International">
       T20I
      </a>
      matches before gaining the status, as
      <a href="/wiki/International_Cricket_Council" title="International Cricket Council">
       ICC
      </a>
      had earlier announced that all matches at the
      <a href="/wiki/2014_ICC_World_Twenty20" title="2014 ICC World Twenty20">
       2014 ICC World Twenty20
      </a>
      would have
      <a href="/wiki/Twenty20_International" title="Twenty20 International">
       T20I
      </a>
      status.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Big_stage_for_two_debutants_188-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Big_stage_for_two_debutants-188">
        [188]
       </a>
      </sup>
      Nepal won the
      <a href="/wiki/2014_ICC_World_Cricket_League_Division_Three" title="2014 ICC World Cricket League Division Three">
       2014 ICC World Cricket League Division Three
      </a>
      held in Malaysia and qualified for the
      <a href="/wiki/2015_ICC_World_Cricket_League_Division_Two" title="2015 ICC World Cricket League Division Two">
       2015 ICC World Cricket League Division Two
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Pun.2C_Malla_and_Budhaayer_shine_as_Nepal_wins_Pepsi_ICC_World_Cricket_League_Division_3_189-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Pun.2C_Malla_and_Budhaayer_shine_as_Nepal_wins_Pepsi_ICC_World_Cricket_League_Division_3-189">
        [189]
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      Nepal finished fourth in the
      <a href="/wiki/2015_ICC_World_Cricket_League_Division_Two" title="2015 ICC World Cricket League Division Two">
       2015 ICC World Cricket League Division Two
      </a>
      in Namibia
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Scorecard_of_3rd_Place_Playoff:_Kenya_v_Nepal.2C_WCL_Division_Two_2015_190-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Scorecard_of_3rd_Place_Playoff:_Kenya_v_Nepal.2C_WCL_Division_Two_2015-190">
        [190]
       </a>
      </sup>
      and qualified for the
      <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9317_ICC_World_Cricket_League_Championship" title="2015–17 ICC World Cricket League Championship">
       2015–17 ICC World Cricket League Championship
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Kenya_and_Nepal_will_take_their_places_in_the_ICC_World_Cricket_League_Championship_191-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Kenya_and_Nepal_will_take_their_places_in_the_ICC_World_Cricket_League_Championship-191">
        [191]
       </a>
      </sup>
      But Nepal failed to secure promotion to Division One and qualification to
      <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9317_ICC_Intercontinental_Cup" title="2015–17 ICC Intercontinental Cup">
       2015–17 ICC Intercontinental Cup
      </a>
      after finishing third in the round-robin stage.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Redemption_for_Netherlands.2C_regret_for_Nepal_192-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Redemption_for_Netherlands.2C_regret_for_Nepal-192">
        [192]
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WCL_Division_Two_2015_Points_Table_193-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-WCL_Division_Two_2015_Points_Table-193">
        [193]
       </a>
      </sup>
      <a href="/wiki/Basanta_Regmi" title="Basanta Regmi">
       Basanta Regmi
      </a>
      became the first bowler to take 100 wickets in the
      <a href="/wiki/World_Cricket_League" title="World Cricket League">
       World Cricket League
      </a>
      . He achieved this feat after taking 2 wickets against
      <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_cricket_team" title="Netherlands national cricket team">
       Netherlands
      </a>
      in the tournament.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Regmi_completes_100_wickets_in_WCL_194-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Regmi_completes_100_wickets_in_WCL-194">
        [194]
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h2>
